#  About this item 
  * 16 Million DIY Colors: Govee smart light bulbs own millions of color and 54 preset scene modes, you can explore your favored one or pick one suits your moods most, bringing yourself a real fantastic lighting experience(Working Voltage: AC 120V). 
  * Music Sync: Our smart light bulbs change color and brightness simultaneously when sounds are detected by the microphone on your phone. Note: only works when the microphone is not occupied. Download Govee Home App and enable microphone permissions. 
  * Smart Control: Govee color changing light bulbs make it possible to control your bulbs with simple voice commands. And you'd also feel free to turn your smart light bulbs on/off, adjust brightness, or change the colors, set scenes via Govee Home App. (Note: Doesn't support 5G) 
  * Group Control: Simplify daily setups by grouping smart bulbs & Govee devices. Create a scheme, add devices, and control them simultaneously. Ensure bulbs are on stable 2.4GHz WiFi for optimal experience. Please Note: This A19 smart bulb cannot be used with smart switches. 
  * Timer and Schedule: Applying the ceiling fan light bulbs to your daily routine now is easier than ever, with timer function and modes like Sunrise & Sunset, you can set your bulbs to brighten when you wake up, and gradually dim when you fall asleep.

[How customer reviews and ratings work](javascript:void\(0\))
Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.
To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.
[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say
Customers find these smart light bulbs to be of good quality, with amazing color options that are easy to change, and appreciate their brightness that can be dimmed well. They are super easy to set up and use on both iPhone and Android devices, and work seamlessly with Alexa and Google Assistant. The connectivity receives mixed feedback - while some customers report easy connectivity, others mention having to reconnect them frequently.

_5 out of 5 stars_
##### Love them!
I love these things, i purchased Govee string lights to put in my living room back in December to replace my old lights that were burning out, and i love those so much i decided to get these when i needed new bulbs for my bedroom lamps! I will say they are still pretty bright even at 1% brightness, so it would be nice to be able to dim them even more, but im having a lot of fun with them. I did struggle to get them paired to the app at first but that was mainly my own issues (app needed updated) and i got confused about the matter hub thing and thought for a bit that i was going to have to return them because i didnt have one. Once i got the app updated they paired right away and ive had no issues with them since!

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ A fantastic value upgrade from LIFX — easier to set up, good performance, and way less hassle ](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/RUB431MT3VB6P/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)
Reviewed in the United States on October 31, 2025
Item Package Quantity: 4[Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)
I picked up two 4-packs of these Govee smart bulbs during a sale to replace a set of aging LIFX bulbs I’ve been using since 2017. After eight years of syncing, grouping, and trying to get everything working just right with LIFX, I finally decided it wasn’t worth the extra cost for features I rarely used. One LIFX bulb had failed, and a couple others were getting flakey with connectivity. I wanted something simpler that still gave me color and scheduling — and Govee delivered.  
  
Setup was incredibly easy. These new bulbs were detected almost instantly when I plugged them in. A couple of taps in the app, and they were connected and even auto-integrated with Alexa. That’s a huge improvement from earlier smart bulb setups (even earlier Govee ones I own). I now have seven of the eight bulbs installed along with two Govee light strips, all grouped and running Halloween scenes on my patio. It’s been a solid setup so far.  
  
Compared to LIFX, the color control and brightness aren’t quite as dynamic. The LIFX strips, especially, had more nuanced transitions and stronger color saturation. But in practice, the difference just doesn’t matter much — especially when synced to music. After years of trying to get light/music syncing to be something magical, I’ve come to realize it’s more of a gimmick than a feature. Govee still delivers good color scenes and effects, and unless you’re obsessive about subtle hue shifts, you’ll be more than satisfied.  
  
I’ve used Govee products for at least five years now — four bulbs and two strips — and they’ve been very reliable. One older bulb has a minor issue where it doesn’t completely turn off and glows faintly like a nightlight. But after that much usage, I’m fine with that. It’s a minor flaw, and the overall track record is solid.  
  
These bulbs have made my smart lighting more manageable. They’re easier to set up than LIFX, play well with Alexa, and give me the features I use most without overcomplicating things. For the price, they’re an excellent value.  
  
Pros:  
• Incredibly easy setup and instant Alexa integration  
• Solid performance with grouping and scenes  
• Very good color options and brightness for the price  
• Great value — especially compared to LIFX  
• Reliable brand experience based on years of use  
  
Cons:  
• LIFX still wins on color precision and transitions  
• One older bulb didn’t fully power off (very minor and after years of use)  
• Music syncing and advanced lighting effects are still mostly gimmicks in both brands  
  
My rating: 5 stars – Product is excellent and exceeds expectations.  
  
Star Rating Guideline:  
• 5 stars – Product is excellent and exceeds expectations. There could be minor issues or stylistic/personal preference mentioned in the review.  
• 4 stars – Very good product. There could be minor issues, but overall this meets expectations.  
• 3 stars – Average. The product works as expected, but does not stand out in any way. I still recommend the product for those that agree with the review and the value the product brings.  
• 2 stars – Significant problems or poor design. Might work for some, but overall not recommendable.  
• 1 star – Serious issues, does not function as expected, misleading, or potentially unsafe.

#####  _5.0 out of 5 stars_ Wonderful lightbulbs!!
Reviewed in Canada on June 10, 2025
Item Package Quantity: 6[Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)
In the past I’ve bought LED light strips and cheap colour changing lightbulbs from Canadian tire- but the strips leave sticky residue (not great when you’re renting!) and are hard to take down, and the cheap lightbulbs had very limited colour options.  
  
A couple months ago we moved to a new home, and I decided to get better light bulbs for our various lamps. I bought these, using 5 of them around our small apartment. The app is pretty intuitive and easy to figure out, and has SO MANY options. Preset colours, warm and cool lighting options, a colour wheel to accurately get any colour you may desire. There are also preset themes that automatically change and cycle through colours (my favourite is “Aurora” that changes colours from bright aqua green to deep blues and purples, simulating the colours of northern lights). You can do so much with these light bulbs and even customize each one to be a different colour if you’d like. We use these every single day in the evenings when we want more ambient light for gaming, relaxing and having company over. Picture doesn’t do it justice, they’re really bright and saturated. You can also choose to make it less saturated and more pastel in the app by playing around with the colour wheel!  
  
10/10 would recommend to everyone!!!

#####  Wonderful lightbulbs!! 
  
Reviewed in Canada on June 10, 2025 
In the past I’ve bought LED light strips and cheap colour changing lightbulbs from Canadian tire- but the strips leave sticky residue (not great when you’re renting!) and are hard to take down, and the cheap lightbulbs had very limited colour options.  
  
A couple months ago we moved to a new home, and I decided to get better light bulbs for our various lamps. I bought these, using 5 of them around our small apartment. The app is pretty intuitive and easy to figure out, and has SO MANY options. Preset colours, warm and cool lighting options, a colour wheel to accurately get any colour you may desire. There are also preset themes that automatically change and cycle through colours (my favourite is “Aurora” that changes colours from bright aqua green to deep blues and purples, simulating the colours of northern lights). You can do so much with these light bulbs and even customize each one to be a different colour if you’d like. We use these every single day in the evenings when we want more ambient light for gaming, relaxing and having company over. Picture doesn’t do it justice, they’re really bright and saturated. You can also choose to make it less saturated and more pastel in the app by playing around with the colour wheel!  
  
10/10 would recommend to everyone!!!

## About this Item
  * 16 Million DIY Colors: Govee smart light bulbs own millions of color and 54 preset scene modes, you can explore your favored one or pick one suits your moods most, bringing yourself a real fantastic lighting experience(Working Voltage: AC 120V).
  * Music Sync: Our smart light bulbs change color and brightness simultaneously when sounds are detected by the microphone on your phone. Note: only works when the microphone is not occupied. Download Govee Home App and enable microphone permissions.
  * Smart Control: Govee color changing light bulbs make it possible to control your bulbs with simple voice commands. And you'd also feel free to turn your smart light bulbs on/off, adjust brightness, or change the colors, set scenes via Govee Home App. (Note: Doesn't support 5G)
  * Group Control: Simplify daily setups by grouping smart bulbs & Govee devices. Create a scheme, add devices, and control them simultaneously. Ensure bulbs are on stable 2.4GHz WiFi for optimal experience. Please Note: This A19 smart bulb cannot be used with smart switches.
  * Timer and Schedule: Applying the ceiling fan light bulbs to your daily routine now is easier than ever, with timer function and modes like Sunrise & Sunset, you can set your bulbs to brighten when you wake up, and gradually dim when you fall asleep.


## Product Description
Govee RGBWW Light Bulbs,Color Changing LED Bulbs Work with Alexa and Google Assistant, Stable Connection LED Light Bulbs( 4Pack) Features Music Sync, these bulbs can changing lighting color with the input voice commands. Voice Control, smart LED bulbs work with Alexa and Google Assistant from distance. Stable Connection, support bluetooth connection, which is more stable than common alexa bulbs. APP Group Control, Group up to 50 smart bulbs and control their features and brightness together. Adjustable Brightness, 1%-100% dimmable brightness can be adjustable via Govee App. Specification Model: H6008 Power: 9W Working Votagle: AC 120V Current: 120mA Screw Base: E26 Color temperature: 2700K-6500K Brightness: 800 lumens Working Temperature: -10℃ to 45℃/14℉ to 114℉ Note The bulb is not waterproof. Avoid exposing it to splashing or dripping water. The operating temperature should be within -10℃ to 45℃/14℉ to 113℉. The bulb's internal light source is unfixable, if it breaks, you must replace the entire bulb. Avoid using the bulbs near heat sources. A WiFi router supporting the 2.4GHz and 802.11b/g/n bands. 5GHz is not supported.
